Users of the current version of the wallets Geth and Parity successfully synchronized, and together with the miners, node operators, as well as business representatives turned out to be in the new network.\n‚úÖAccording to the parameters incorporated in the update, the block creation time should return to 15 seconds after it has grown to 20 seconds due to the activation of the complexity bomb. In addition, miners will now be able to mine about 13,400 ETH per day, and developers will have access to improved network capabilities.\nA few minutes before the update and some time after it, the portal tracking the fork was not working, but no problems were noticed on the network itself.\nüî•üî•üî•üî•üî•üî•üî•üî•üî•üî•üî•üî•üî•üî•üî•\n #–≠—Ñ–∏—Ä–∏—É–º #—Ö–∞—Ä–¥—Ñ–æ—Ä–∫ #Constantinople #Metropolis #–æ–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è #–º–∞–π–Ω–∏–Ω–≥ #Ethereum #ETH",

This was announced yesterday by the operator of the Stuttgart Stock Exchange. The developer was her unit Sowa Labs.\nüîΩ It is noted that at the moment the novelty is available only to users from Germany, but in the future it will spread to other countries. For the time being, traders will be able to use Bison daily only from 6 am local time until midnight. In the Stuttgart Stock Exchange noted that the application has a news feed that uses artificial intelligence. In addition, users do not need to set up a wallet for trading. This is due to the fact that a subsidiary of Boerse Stuttgart - Blocknox, acts as a repository for users of the application, using the escrow system.\n‚ÄúHead of Sowa Labs, Ulli Spankowski, said that developers are planning to make money on price spreads.‚Äù Blocknox, another division of the Stuttgart Stock Exchange, will be responsible for storing the assets. application, through which users can use the functions of the wallet without connecting to a computer.\n‚úÖThe application called Ledger Live was previously only available for personal computers, but now it has been launched for mobile devices. With it, users of the new wallet Ledger Nano X will be able to use all the functions of the wallet using a Bluetooth connection.\nRepresentatives of the company noted that at the moment the application is targeted specifically at users of Ledger Nano X, but the owners of Nano S and Blue can only check the balance on their device. In the future, however, users of old models will also be able to use all the functions of the device from a mobile phone. For Nano S, you will have to use an OTG USB adapter, and all functions will be available only on Android OS.\n‚ùóÔ∏è Note that the interface of the Ledger application is very similar to that of a competitor, Trezor Bridge, which was released last year. However, all the functionality of Trezor devices is available only on personal computers, and only a limited list of operations can be performed from a mobile phone.\n‚òù Recall that at the end of last year, at the 35C3 Refreshing Memories conference, researchers announced the possibility of hacking into the hardware wallets Ledger Nano S and Ledger Blue. (USD) Daily Future‚Äù and will cost 1 BTC. The contract will be calculated in US dollars. The minimum price fluctuation will be $ 2.50 for one contract; however, for large transactions from ten contracts, it will be possible to determine the price with an accuracy of up to $ 0.01. There are no daily restrictions on price fluctuations, but a limit of 100,000 lots has been set. Commission for exchange and clearing services will be $ 0.50 for each participant in the transaction.\nFor the purpose of technical implementation of trade, listing of new contracts will be held every day. Trading will be conducted from 8:00 pm to 6:00 pm the following day, New York time. Preliminary opening of the auction will be carried out at 19:55, and calculations will be made from 16:58 to 17:00.\nüîΩ Obviously, the Bakkt platform is ready to start trading, but has to wait for permission from the US Commodity Futures Trading Commission (CFTC). security problems‚ùóÔ∏è\n‚ö°Ô∏è‚ö°Ô∏è‚ö°Ô∏è‚ö°Ô∏è‚ö°Ô∏è‚ö°Ô∏è‚ö°Ô∏è‚ö°Ô∏è‚ö°Ô∏è‚ö°Ô∏è‚ö°Ô∏è‚ö°Ô∏è‚ö°Ô∏è‚ö°Ô∏è‚ö°Ô∏è\n The long-awaited update of Constantinople Ethereum was postponed after a critical vulnerability was discovered in one of the planned changes. The company ChainSecurity, which is engaged in the audit of smart contracts, said on Tuesday that the proposal to improve Ethereum (EIP) No. 1283, if implemented, could provide an attacker with a loophole in the code to steal users' funds.\n‚úÖDuring the teleconference, Ethereum developers, as well as client developers and other network projects, agreed to postpone hardfork for at least as long as they evaluate the problem. Among the participants of the teleconference were the creator of Ethereum Vitalik Buterin, the developers Hudson Jameson, Nick Johnson and Evan Van Ness, as well as the product manager Parity Afri Schoedon.\n–ëWhen discussing the vulnerability, the project developers came to the conclusion that the correction of the error will take too much time and cannot be implemented before the hard forks, which was scheduled for 04:00 UTC on January 17th. The new date of the hardfork will be determined during the regular teleconference of Ethereum developers on Friday.\n‚òù A vulnerability called a re-entry attack allows an attacker to re-access the same function several times without informing the user. Last week, the exchange has already added support for perpetual swaps on BCH, so 4 types of such contracts are now available on it.\nPerpetual swaps operate on the principle of futures contracts, but with unlimited validity and the possibility of closing at any time. Swaps allow traders to open both short and long positions, speculating on the dynamic of the course.\n‚úÖ For BCH, ETH and EOS swaps, a leverage ratio of up to 40x is available. In addition, each contract is equivalent to $ 10. To determine the price of swaps, data from several exchanges are used. Traders can leverage up to 100x, and the value of such a contract is $ 100.\nOK About OKEx plans to add new perpetual contracts became known in early December. Then it was assumed that they will be available from December 11.
